         <h2 class="flo-article-head__heading">How to make and receive hands-free calls with SYNC</h2>
         <div class="vehicle-selector">
          <script>

        <div data-article-mask=""> 
         <div class="card-header header">
          <div class="flo-article-hero "> 
           <div class="flo-article-hero__media flo-hide-print"> 
            <img src="/content/dam/assets/ford/how-tos/sync-technology/using-phone/make-and-receive-hands-free-calls/d-ford-hands-free-calling.jpg" class="flo-article-hero__image flo-article-hero__image--large" alt="Ford SYNC Voice Command"> 
            <img src="/content/dam/assets/ford/how-tos/sync-technology/using-phone/make-and-receive-hands-free-calls/m-ford-hands-free-calling.jpg" class="flo-article-hero__image flo-article-hero__image--small" alt="Ford SYNC Voice Command"> 
           </div> 
           <!-- Share links --> 
           <div class="flo-article-hero__share flo-hide-print" data-share-buttons="true" data-url="https://owner.ford.com/how-tos/sync-technology/sync/phone/how-to-make-and-receive-hands-free-calls-with-sync.html" data-title="How to make and receive hands-free calls with SYNC | SYNC | Official Ford Owner Site" data-description="Learn how to make and receive hands-free calling with Ford SYNC. Follow these 5 steps to get your Bluetooth phone paired with SYNC with MYFord Touch. 
" data-template-type="grid"></div> 
           <div class="flo-article-hero__desc"> 
            <p>Once your Bluetooth<sup></sup>-enabled phone is paired with and connected to SYNC<sup></sup>, you can answer a call by touching a button. Transfer your phonebook to SYNC and use simple voice commands to call any of your contacts by name and location, like "Call Mary at office."<sup>27,48</sup></p> 
           </div> 
          </div>
         </div> 
         <div class="flo-article-body"> 
          <div class="tile-container-parsys tiles">
           <div class="step-by-step-tile section">
            <div class="flo-step-list"> 
             <div class="slides">
              <li class="flo-step-list__item section">
               <div class="subtile-intro">
                <h3 class="flo-step-list__title">Before you start</h3>
                <p class="flo-step-list__lead-in">There are a few things you should do before starting step 1:</p>
               </div> 
               <div class="flo-step-list__details"> 
                <div class="flo-step-list__copy flo-step-list__copy--full flo-rich-text"> 
                 <ul> 
                  <li>Make sure that your phone is compatible with SYNC by checking our <a href="/how-tos/sync-technology/all/phone/phones-compatible-with-sync.html">compatibility chart</a>&nbsp;</li> 
                  <li>Pair your phone to SYNC and download your phonebook&nbsp;</li> 
                  <li>Familiarize yourself with the <a href="/how-tos/sync-technology/sync/setup/learn-the-controls-for-sync.html">controls in your vehicle</a>&nbsp;</li> 
                  <li>If youd like to call contacts by name, be sure you<a href="/how-tos/sync-technology/sync/phone/how-to-transfer-your-phonebook-to-sync.html"> transfer your phonebook to SYNC</a></li> 
                 </ul> 
                </div> 
               </div> </li> 
              <li class="flo-step-list__item section">
               <div class="flo-step-list__details"> 
                <div class="flo-step-list__copy flo-step-list__copy--full flo-rich-text"> 
                 <p>To make a hands-free call, press or pull the <strong>Voice</strong> button.</p> 
                 <p><br> Youll hear a tone that indicates SYNC is listening. SYNC may prompt, SYNC. Please say a command.</p>
                </div> 
               </div> </li> 
              <li class="flo-step-list__item section">
               <div class="flo-step-list__details"> 
                <div class="flo-step-list__copy flo-step-list__copy--full flo-rich-text"> 
                 <p><b>Say Phone.</b> After SYNC confirms it has heard you, say one of the following:<br> &nbsp;</p> 
                 <p>Dial &lt;after system responds with "number please," say the number&gt;</p> 
                 <p>Call &lt;name of contact as its listed in your phonebook&gt;</p> 
                 <p>Call &lt;name of contact and location as its listed in your phonebook&gt;</p> 
                 <div>
                  &nbsp;
                 </div> 
                 <p>SYNC may prompt you to confirm the number or the name and location of your contact.</p> 
                </div> 
               </div> </li> 
              <li class="flo-step-list__item section">
               <div class="flo-step-list__details"> 
                <div class="flo-step-list__copy flo-step-list__copy--full flo-rich-text"> 
                 <p><strong>Say your choice</strong> to confirm your selection. When your call is answered, begin speaking.</p>
                </div> 
               </div> </li> 
              <li class="flo-step-list__item section">
               <div class="flo-step-list__details"> 
                <div class="flo-step-list__copy flo-step-list__copy--full flo-rich-text"> 
                 <p>To end your call, press and hold the <strong>Phone</strong>&nbsp;or<strong> End Call</strong>&nbsp;button for a few seconds.</p>
                </div> 
               </div> </li> 
              <li class="flo-step-list__item section">
               <div class="flo-step-list__details"> 
                <div class="flo-step-list__copy flo-step-list__copy--full flo-rich-text"> 
                 <p>To receive a hands-free call, press the <strong>Phone </strong>or<strong> Call Answer</strong>&nbsp;button and begin speaking.</p> 
                 <p><br> If you choose to ignore the call, it will be logged as a missed call.</p>
                </div> 
               </div> </li> 
             </div> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
           <div class="quick-tip-tile section">
            <div class="flo-callout"> 
             <div class="flo-callout__header"> 
              <div class="flo-callout__icon flo-icon-SF_quick-tip"></div> 
              <h3 class="flo-callout__header-title">Quick Tip</h3> 
             </div> 
             <div class="flo-callout__body"> 
              <div class="flo-callout__copy flo-callout__copy--"> 
               <div class="flo-callout__desc flo-rich-text"> 
                <h3>Continuing a call when you get in or out of your vehicle</h3> 
                <p>If youre on a call while getting into your vehicle, and your phone is already paired, simply turn on your vehicle. The call will transfer automatically to SYNC.</p> 
                <p><br> If you want to continue your call as you get out of your vehicle, turn off your vehicle and open the door. The call will transfer automatically to your phone. If you stay in your vehicle in Park, the 10-minute-accessory-delay feature will keep the call connected for 10 minutes, or until a door is opened.</p>
               </div> 
              </div> 
             </div> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
          </div>
